00309     // connecte le widget dial_buttons à la fenêtre de configuration
00310     // Cliquer sur le boutton Ok dans cette fenêtre emet un signet accepted() qui est reçu par la fenêtre de configuration.
00311     // Cette fenêtre modale va se fermer et renvoyer la valeur true pour le boolléen result_settings_window. Les changements de paramètres seront effectués.
00312     connect( dial_buttons, SIGNAL(accepted()), settings_window, SLOT(accept()) );
00313     // Cliquer sur le boutton Cancel dans cette fenêtre emet un signet rejected() qui est reçu par la fenêtre de configuration.
00314     // Cette fenêtre modale va se fermer et renvoyer la valeur false pour le boolléen result_settings_window. Les changements de paramètres ne seront pas effectués.
00315     connect( dial_buttons, SIGNAL(rejected()), settings_window, SLOT(reject()) );
00316 
00317     connect( dial_buttons->button(QDialogButtonBox::Reset), SIGNAL(clicked()), this, SLOT(default_settings()) );

01534 
01535 void ImageViewer::print()
01536 {
01537     Q_ASSERT(&(imageLabel->get_qimage()));
01538 #ifndef QT_NO_PRINTER
01539     QPrintDialog dialog(&printer, this);
01540     if( dialog.exec() )
01541     {
01542         QPainter painter(&printer);
01543         QRect rect = painter.viewport();
01544         QSize size = (&(imageLabel->get_qimage()))->size();
01545         size.scale(rect.size(), Qt::KeepAspectRatio);
01546         painter.setViewport(rect.x(), rect.y(), size.width(), size.height());
01547         painter.setWindow((&(imageLabel->get_qimage()))->rect());
01548         painter.drawImage(0, 0, *(&(imageLabel->get_qimage())));
01549     }
01550 #endif
01551 }

01571 
01572 // Fonction appelée pour effectuer la segmentation
01573 void ImageViewer::start()
01574 {
01575 
01576     startAct->setEnabled(false);
01577     openAct->setEnabled(false);
01578     stopAct->setEnabled(true);
01579 
01580     // variables pour les évenements clic droit et clic gauche de la souris
01581     hasClickStopping = false;
01582 
01583     if( img1 != NULL )
01584     {
01585         // Filtre
01586 
01587         // création objet en statique
01588         //Filters filters1(img1, img_height, img_width);
01589 
01590         // création objet dynamique (permet de recupérer filtered depuis la fonction MouseMooveEvent)
01591         // evite copie d'un buffer
01592         if( filters1 != NULL )
01593         {
01594             delete filters1;
01595             filters1 = NULL;
01596         }
01597 
01598         if( filtersRGB1 != NULL )
01599         {
01600             delete filtersRGB1;
01601             filtersRGB1 = NULL;
01602         }
01603 
01604         const unsigned char* img1_filtered;
01605 
01606         if( !isRgb1 )
01607         {
01608             filters1 = new ofeli::Filters(img1, img_width, img_height);
01609 
01610             if( hasPreprocess )
01611             {
01612                 if( hasGaussianNoise )
01613                 {
01614                     filters1->gaussian_white_noise(std_noise);
01615                 }
01616                 if( hasSaltNoise )
01617                 {
01618                     filters1->salt_pepper_noise(proba_noise);
01619                 }
01620                 if( hasSpeckleNoise )
01621                 {
01622                     filters1->speckle(std_speckle_noise);
01623                 }
01624 
01625                 if( hasMeanFilt )
01626                 {
01627                     filters1->mean_filtering(kernel_mean_length1);
01628                 }
01629                 if( hasGaussianFilt )
01630                 {
01631                     filters1->gaussian_filtering(kernel_gaussian_length1, sigma);
01632                 }
01633 
01634                 if( hasMedianFilt )
01635                 {
01636                     if( hasO1algo1 )
01637                     {
01638                         filters1->median_filtering_o1(kernel_median_length1);
01639                     }
01640                     else
01641                     {
01642                         filters1->median_filtering_oNlogN(kernel_median_length1);
01643                     }
01644                 }
01645                 if( hasAnisoDiff )
01646                 {
01647                     filters1->anisotropic_diffusion(max_itera1, lambda1, kappa1, aniso_option1);
01648                 }  
01649                 if( hasOpenFilt )
01650                 {
01651                     if( hasO1morpho1 )
01652                     {
01653                         filters1->opening_o1(kernel_open_length1);
01654                     }
01655                     else
01656                     {
01657                         filters1->opening(kernel_open_length1);
01658                     }
01659                 }
01660                 if( hasCloseFilt )
01661                 {
01662                     if( hasO1morpho1 )
01663                     {
01664                         filters1->closing_o1(kernel_close_length1);
01665                     }
01666                     else
01667                     {
01668                         filters1->closing(kernel_close_length1);
01669                     }
01670                 }
01671                 if( hasTophatFilt )
01672                 {
01673                     if( isWhiteTophat )
01674                     {
01675                         if( hasO1morpho1 )
01676                         {
01677                             filters1->white_top_hat_o1(kernel_tophat_length1);
01678                         }
01679                         else
01680                         {
01681                             filters1->white_top_hat(kernel_tophat_length1);
01682                         }
01683                     }
01684                     else
01685                     {
01686                         if( hasO1morpho1 )

02348                             image_result_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
02349                         }
02350                     }
02351                 }
02352 
02353                 else
02354                 {
02355                     for( ofeli::List::const_Link iterator = Lout1->get_begin(); !iterator->end(); iterator = iterator->get_next() )
02356                     {
02357                         i = 3*iterator->get_elem();
02358 
02359                         image_result_uchar[i] = img1_filtered[i];
02360                         image_result_uchar[i+1] = img1_filtered[i+1];
02361                         image_result_uchar[i+2] = img1_filtered[i+2];
02362                     }
02363 
02364                     for( ofeli::List::const_Link iterator = Lin1->get_begin(); !iterator->end(); iterator = iterator->get_next() )
02365                     {
02366                         i = 3*iterator->get_elem();
02367 
02368                         image_result_uchar[i] = img1_filtered[i];
02369                         image_result_uchar[i+1] = img1_filtered[i+1];
02370                         image_result_uchar[i+2] = img1_filtered[i+2];
02371                     }
02372                 }
02373 
02374                 if( model == 1 )
02375                 {
02376                     if( !isRgb1 )
02377                     {
02378                         acWithoutEdges1->evolve_one_iteration();
02379                         Lout1 = &acWithoutEdges1->get_Lout();
02380                         Lin1 = &acWithoutEdges1->get_Lin();
02381 
02382                         iterations1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_iterations();
02383                         hasAlgoStopping1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_hasAlgoStopping();
02384 
02385                         // pour l'affichage
02386                         Cout1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cout();
02387                         Cin1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cin();
02388                         RGBout = QColor(Cout1,Cout1,Cout1);
02389                         RGBin = QColor(Cin1,Cin1,Cin1);
02390                         Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(Cout1));
02391                         Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(Cin1));
02392                     }
02393                     else
02394                     {
02395                         acWithoutEdgesYUV1->evolve_one_iteration();
02396                         Lout1 = &acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lout();
02397                         Lin1 = &acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lin();
02398 
02399                         iterations1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_iterations();
02400                         hasAlgoStopping1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_hasAlgoStopping();
02401 
02402                         CoutR = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutR();
02403                         CoutG = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutG();
02404                         CoutB = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutB();
02405 
02406                         CinR = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinR();
02407                         CinG = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinG();
02408                         CinB = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinB();
02409 
02410                         RGBout = QColor(CoutR,CoutG,CoutB);
02411                         RGBin = QColor(CinR,CinG,CinB);
02412 
02413                         Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CoutR)+","+QString::number(CoutG)+","+QString::number(CoutB)+")");
02414                         Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CinR)+","+QString::number(CinB)+","+QString::number(CinB)+")");
02415                     }
02416                 }
02417                 if( model == 2 )
02418                 {
02419                     geodesicAc1->evolve_one_iteration();
02420                     Lout1 = &geodesicAc1->get_Lout();
02421                     Lin1 = &geodesicAc1->get_Lin();
02422 
02423                     iterations1 = geodesicAc1->get_iterations();
02424                     hasAlgoStopping1 = geodesicAc1->get_hasAlgoStopping();
02425                     // pour l'affichage
02426                     otsu_threshold1 = geodesicAc1->get_otsu_threshold();
02427                     threshold_text->setText(tr("Otsu's threshold of gradient = ")+QString::number(otsu_threshold1));
02428                 }
02429 
02430                 text->setText("<font color=green>"+tr("iterations (≤")+QString::number(max_iterations1)+") = "+QString::number(iterations1));
02431 
02432                 // marque les contours dans la QImage
02433                 for( ofeli::List::const_Link iterator = Lout1->get_begin(); !iterator->end(); iterator = iterator->get_next() )
02434                 {
02435                     i = 3*iterator->get_elem();
02436 
02437                     image_result_uchar[i] = Rout1;
02438                     image_result_uchar[i+1] = Gout1;
02439                     image_result_uchar[i+2] = Bout1;
02440                 }
02441 
02442                 for( ofeli::List::const_Link iterator = Lin1->get_begin(); !iterator->end(); iterator = iterator->get_next() )
02443                 {
02444                     i = 3*iterator->get_elem();
02445 
02446                     image_result_uchar[i] = Rin1;
02447                     image_result_uchar[i+1] = Gin1;
02448                     image_result_uchar[i+2] = Bin1;
02449 
02450                 }
02451 
02452                 // Pour afficher plusieurs fois dans une boucle
02453                 QApplication::processEvents();
02454                 // Affichage
02455                 imageLabel->update();
02456                 infinite_loop();
02457             } while (!hasAlgoStopping1);
02458 
02459             // Temps d'exécution de la boucle do-while
02460             stopTime = clock();
02461             elapsedTime = (stopTime - startTime) / double(CLOCKS_PER_SEC);
02462             QApplication::processEvents();
02463             time_text->setText(tr("time = ")+QString::number(elapsedTime)+" s");
02464         }
02465         // on affiche rien du tout pour evaluer le temps de calcul
02466         // if( !hasDisplayEach )
02467         else
02468         {
02469             // Pour calculer le temps d'exécution
02470             double elapsedTime;
02471             clock_t stopTime, startTime;
02472 
02473             startTime = clock();
02474 
02475             if( model == 1 )
02476             {
02477                 if( !isRgb1 )
02478                 {
02479                     acWithoutEdges1->evolve_to_final_state();
02480                     Lout1 = &acWithoutEdges1->get_Lout();
02481                     Lin1 = &acWithoutEdges1->get_Lin();
02482                 }
02483                 else
02484                 {
02485                     acWithoutEdgesYUV1->evolve_to_final_state();
02486                     Lout1 = &acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lout();
02487                     Lin1 = &acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lin();
02488                 }
02489             }
02490             if( model == 2 )
02491             {
02492                 geodesicAc1->evolve_to_final_state();
02493                 Lout1 = &geodesicAc1->get_Lout();
02494                 Lin1 = &geodesicAc1->get_Lin();
02495             }
02496 
02497             // Temps d'exécution de la boucle do-while
02498             stopTime = clock();
02499             elapsedTime = (stopTime - startTime) / double(CLOCKS_PER_SEC);
02500             QApplication::processEvents();
02501             time_text->setText(tr("time = ")+QString::number(elapsedTime)+" s");
02502         }
02503 
02504         if( model == 1 )
02505         {
02506             if( !isRgb1 )
02507             {
02508                 iterations1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_iterations();
02509                 hasListsChanges1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_hasListsChanges();
02510                 hasOscillation1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_hasOscillation();
02511 
02512                 Cout1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cout();
02513                 Cin1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cin();
02514                 RGBout = QColor(Cout1,Cout1,Cout1);
02515                 RGBin = QColor(Cin1,Cin1,Cin1);
02516                 Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(Cout1));
02517                 Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(Cin1));
02518             }
02519             else
02520             {
02521                 iterations1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_iterations();
02522                 hasListsChanges1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_hasListsChanges();
02523                 hasOscillation1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_hasOscillation();
02524 
02525                 CoutR = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutR();
02526                 CoutG = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutG();
02527                 CoutB = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutB();
02528 
02529                 CinR = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinR();
02530                 CinG = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinG();
02531                 CinB = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinB();
02532 
02533                 RGBout = QColor(CoutR,CoutG,CoutB);
02534                 RGBin = QColor(CinR,CinG,CinB);
02535 
02536                 Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CoutR)+","+QString::number(CoutG)+","+QString::number(CoutB)+")");
02537                 Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CinR)+","+QString::number(CinG)+","+QString::number(CinB)+")");
02538             }
02539         }
02540         if( model == 2 )
02541         {
02542             iterations1 = geodesicAc1->get_iterations();
02543             hasListsChanges1 = geodesicAc1->get_hasListsChanges();
02544             hasOscillation1 = geodesicAc1->get_hasOscillation();
02545         }
02546 
02547         QApplication::processEvents();
02548         if( !hasListsChanges1 )
02549         {
02550             changes_text->setText("<font color=red>"+tr("lists changes = false"));
02551         }
02552         
02553         if( hasOscillation1 )
02554         {
02555             oscillation_text->setText("<font color=red>"+tr("oscillation = true"));
02556         }
02557         
02558         if( iterations1 >= max_iterations1 )
02559         {
02560             text->setText("<font color=red>"+tr("iterations (≤")+QString::number(max_iterations1)+") = "+QString::number(iterations1));
02561         }
02562         else
02563         {
02564             text->setText("<font color=green>"+tr("iterations (≤")+QString::number(max_iterations1)+") = "+QString::number(iterations1));
02565         }
02566 
02567         wait(seconds_wait/2.0);
02568         if( hasStepByStep )
02569         {
02570             hasClickStopping = true;
02571         }
02572         infinite_loop();
02573 
02575         // affiche une fois le contour actif avec l'image initiale en dessous
02577 
02578         if( hasAlgoBreaking )
02579         {
02580             hasAlgoBreaking = false;
02581             startAct->setEnabled(true);
02582             openAct->setEnabled(true);
02583             stopAct->setEnabled(false);
02584             return;
02585         }
02586 
02587         // marque les contours
02588         for( ofeli::List::const_Link iterator = Lout1->get_begin(); !iterator->end(); iterator = iterator->get_next() )
02589         {
02590             i = 3*iterator->get_elem();
02591 
02592             image_uchar[i] = Rout1;
02593             image_uchar[i+1] = Gout1;
02594             image_uchar[i+2] = Bout1;
02595         }
02596 
02597         for( ofeli::List::const_Link iterator = Lin1->get_begin(); !iterator->end(); iterator = iterator->get_next() )
02598         {
02599             i = 3*iterator->get_elem();
02600 
02601             image_uchar[i] = Rin1;
02602             image_uchar[i+1] = Gin1;
02603             image_uchar[i+2] = Bin1;
02604         }
02605 
02606         image_disp = 1;
02607 
02608         // Affichage
02609         imageLabel->set_qimage(image);
02610 
02612         // fin de
02614 
02615         hasResultDisp = true;
02616 
02617         openAct->setEnabled(true);
02618     }
02619     hasStepByStep = false;
02620     startAct->setEnabled(true);
02621     stopAct->setEnabled(false);
02622 
02623 }
02624 
02625 void ImageViewer::wait(double seconds)
02626 {
02627   QApplication::processEvents();
02628 
02629   clock_t endwait;
02630   endwait = clock()+seconds *CLOCKS_PER_SEC ;
02631   while( clock() < endwait )
02632   {
02633   }
02634 }

02733

02735 
02736     fileMenu->addSeparator();
02737 
02738     fileMenu->addAction(saveAct);
02739     fileMenu->addAction(printAct);
02740     fileMenu->addSeparator();
02741     fileMenu->addAction(exitAct);
02742 
02743     updateRecentFileActions();
02744 
02745     viewMenu = new QMenu(tr("&View"), this);
02746     viewMenu->addAction(zoomInAct);
02747     viewMenu->addAction(zoomOutAct);
02748     viewMenu->addAction(normalSizeAct);
02749 
02750     segmentationMenu = new QMenu(tr("&Segmentation"), this);
02751     segmentationMenu->addAction(startAct);

02760     //helpMenu->addAction(aboutQtAct);
02761

02764     menuBar()->addMenu(segmentationMenu);

02767 
02768 // Fonction d'origine, modifiée pour le changement d'echelle de l'image
02769 void ImageViewer::scaleImage(double factor)
02770 {
02771     Q_ASSERT(imageLabel->pixmap());
02772     scaleFactor *= factor;
02773     imageLabel->resize(scaleFactor * imageLabel->pixmap()->size());
02774 
02775     // ajout de code, pour récuperer les infos lors d'un zoom pour la segmentation
02777 
02778     adjustScrollBar(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(), factor);
02779     adjustScrollBar(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(), factor);
02780 
02781     zoomInAct->setEnabled(scaleFactor < 3.0);
02782     zoomOutAct->setEnabled(scaleFactor > 0.333);
02783 }
02784 
02785 void ImageViewer::adjustScrollBar(QScrollBar *scrollBar, double factor)
02786 {
02787     scrollBar->setValue(int(factor * scrollBar->value()
02788                             + ((factor - 1) * scrollBar->pageStep()/2)));
02789 }

02799 // Création du layout pour l'onglet algorithm de la fenêtre de configuration
02800 QVBoxLayout *ImageViewer::algorithm()
02801 {
02802     // création de 3 groupbox pour l'onglet algorithm
02803 
02806 
02807     QGroupBox* externalspeed_groupbox = new QGroupBox(tr("Cycle 1 : data dependant evolution"));
02808 
02809     Na_spin = new QSpinBox;
02810     Na_spin->setSingleStep(1);
02811     Na_spin->setMinimum(1);
02812     Na_spin->setMaximum(999);
02813     Na_spin->setSuffix(tr(" iterations"));
02814     Na_spin->setToolTip(tr("iterations in the cycle 1, active contour penetrability"));
02815     QFormLayout *Na_layout = new QFormLayout;
02816     Na_layout->addRow("Na =", Na_spin);
02817     if( operating_system == 2 )
02818     {
02819         Na_layout->setFormAlignment(Qt::AlignLeft);
02820     }
02821 
02822     klength_gradient_spin = new QSpinBox;
02823     klength_gradient_spin->setSingleStep(2);
02824     klength_gradient_spin->setMinimum(1);
02825     klength_gradient_spin->setMaximum(499);
02826 
02827     chanvese_radio = new QRadioButton(tr("Chan-Vese model"));
02828     chanvese_radio->setToolTip(tr("region-based model for bimodal images"));
02829 
02830     lambda_out_spin = new QSpinBox;
02831     lambda_out_spin->setSingleStep(1);
02832     lambda_out_spin->setMinimum(0);
02833     lambda_out_spin->setMaximum(100000);
02834     lambda_out_spin->setToolTip(tr("weight of the outside homogeneity criterion"));
02835 
02836     lambda_in_spin = new QSpinBox;
02837     lambda_in_spin->setSingleStep(1);
02838     lambda_in_spin->setMinimum(0);
02839     lambda_in_spin->setMaximum(100000);
02840     lambda_in_spin->setToolTip(tr("weight of the inside homogeneity criterion"));
02841 
02842     QFormLayout* lambda_layout = new QFormLayout;
02843     QSettings settings;
02844     Rout1 = (unsigned char)(settings.value("Settings/Display/Rout", 0).toInt());
02845     Gout1 = (unsigned char)(settings.value("Settings/Display/Gout", 0).toInt());
02846     Bout1 = (unsigned char)(settings.value("Settings/Display/Bout", 255).toInt());
02847     Rin1 = (unsigned char)(settings.value("Settings/Display/Rin", 255).toInt());
02848     Gin1 = (unsigned char)(settings.value("Settings/Display/Gin", 0).toInt());
02849     Bin1 = (unsigned char)(settings.value("Settings/Display/Bin", 0).toInt());
02850     QColor RGBout_list(Rout1,Gout1,Bout1);
02851     QColor RGBin_list(Rin1,Gin1,Bin1);
02852     lambda_layout->addRow("<font color="+RGBout_list.name()+">"+"λout"+"<font color=black>"+" =", lambda_out_spin);
02853     lambda_layout->addRow("<font color="+RGBin_list.name()+">"+"λin"+"<font color=black>"+" =", lambda_in_spin);
02854     if( operating_system == 2 )
02855     {
02856         lambda_layout->setFormAlignment(Qt::AlignLeft);
02857     }
02858 
02859     QVBoxLayout* chanvese_layout = new QVBoxLayout;
02860     chanvese_layout->addWidget(chanvese_radio);
02861     chanvese_layout->addLayout(lambda_layout);
02862 
02863     geodesic_radio = new QRadioButton(tr("geodesic model"));
02864     geodesic_radio->setToolTip(tr("edge-based model for smoothed multimodal images"));
02865 
02866     klength_gradient_spin = new QSpinBox;
02867     klength_gradient_spin->setSingleStep(2);
02868     klength_gradient_spin->setMinimum(1);
02869     klength_gradient_spin->setMaximum(499);
02870     klength_gradient_spin->setSuffix("²");
02871     klength_gradient_spin->setToolTip(tr("morphological gradient structuring element size"));
02872     QFormLayout *gradient_layout = new QFormLayout;
02873     gradient_layout->addRow(tr("SE size ="), klength_gradient_spin);
02874     if( operating_system == 2 )
02875     {
02876         gradient_layout->setFormAlignment(Qt::AlignLeft);
02877     }
02878     connect(klength_gradient_spin,SIGNAL(valueChanged(int)),this,SLOT(filtering_visu()));
02879 
02880     QVBoxLayout* geodesic_layout = new QVBoxLayout;
02881     geodesic_layout->addWidget(geodesic_radio);
02882     geodesic_layout->addLayout(gradient_layout);
02883 
02884     QHBoxLayout* speed_layout = new QHBoxLayout;
02885     speed_layout->addLayout(chanvese_layout);
02886     speed_layout->addLayout(geodesic_layout);
02887 
02888     yuv_groupbox = new QGroupBox(tr("normalized (Y,U,V) color space weighting"));
02889     yuv_groupbox->setFlat(true);
02890 
02891     Yspin = new QSpinBox;
02892     Yspin->setSingleStep(1);
02893     Yspin->setMinimum(0);
02894     Yspin->setMaximum(100000);
02895     Yspin->setToolTip(tr("luminance weight"));
02896 
02897     Uspin = new QSpinBox;
02898     Uspin->setSingleStep(1);
02899     Uspin->setMinimum(0);
02900     Uspin->setMaximum(100000);
02901     Uspin->setToolTip(tr("chrominance weight"));
02902 
02903     Vspin = new QSpinBox;
02904     Vspin->setSingleStep(1);
02905     Vspin->setMinimum(0);
02906     Vspin->setMaximum(100000);
02907     Vspin->setToolTip(tr("chrominance weight"));
02908 
02909     connect(Yspin,SIGNAL(valueChanged(int)),this,SLOT(filtering_visu()));
02910     connect(Uspin,SIGNAL(valueChanged(int)),this,SLOT(filtering_visu()));
02911     connect(Vspin,SIGNAL(valueChanged(int)),this,SLOT(filtering_visu()));
02912 
02913     QFormLayout* yuv_layout = new QFormLayout;
02914     yuv_layout->addRow(tr("Y weight ="), Yspin);
02915     yuv_layout->addRow(tr("U weight ="), Uspin);

03690 
03691 // Fonction appelée lors de l'ouverture de la fenêtre de configuration et valider ou refuser les changements
03692 void ImageViewer::settings()
03693 {
03694     if( onglets->currentIndex() == 1 )
03695     {
03696         filtering_visu();
03697         phi_visu(true);
03698         shape_visu();
03699     }
03700     else
03701     {
03702         filtering_visu();
03703         phi_visu(false);
03704     }
03705 
03706     // on s'assure que la fenêtre de configuration n'est pas déja affichée
03707     if( settings_window->isVisible() )
03708     {
03709         QMessageBox::critical(this, tr("Error"), tr("Close settings window before."));
03710     }
03711     else
03712     {
03713         // booléen permettant de savoir si l'utilisateur accepte ou rejette les réglages de la fenêtre de configuration
03714         int result_settings_window;
03715 
03716         // la méthode exec() permet d'afficher la fenêtre de configuration settings_window de maniere modale,
03717         // de plus cette méthode retourne un booléen en fonction de l'acceptation ou du rejet des réglages
03718         result_settings_window = settings_window->exec();
03719 
03720         // la méthode show() permet d'afficher la fenêtre de configuration mais de maniere non modale,
03721         //  ne renvoie pas de booléen
03722         //settings_window->show();
03723 
03724         if( result_settings_window )
03725         {
03726             // Ok = les variables vont prendre leur valeur en fonction de l'état des widgets de la fenêtre de configuration
03727             apply_settings();
03728 
03729         }
03730         else
03731         {
03732             // Annuler = les widgets vont reprendre leur état en fonction des valeurs des variables
03733             cancel_settings();
03734         }
03735     }
03736 }
03737 
03738 // si on clique sur le boutton Ok de settings_window
03739 // les paramètres prennent leurs valeurs en fonction de l'état des widgets
03740 void ImageViewer::apply_settings()
03741 {

04075         Bout1 = 255;
04076     }
04077     if( outsidecolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 4 )
04078     {
04079         Rout1 = 255;
04080         Gout1 = 0;
04081         Bout1 = 255;
04082     }
04083     if( outsidecolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 5 )
04084     {
04085         Rout1 = 255;
04086         Gout1 = 255;
04087         Bout1 = 0;
04088     }
04089     if( outsidecolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 6 )
04090     {
04091         Rout1 = 0;
04092         Gout1 = 0;
04093         Bout1 = 0;
04094     }
04095     if( outsidecolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 7 )
04096     {
04097         Rout1 = 255;
04098         Gout1 = 255;
04099         Bout1 = 255;
04100     }
04101 
04102     if( outsidecolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 8 )
04103     {
04104         Rout1 = Rout_selected1;
04105         Gout1 = Gout_selected1;
04106         Bout1 = Bout_selected1;
04107     }
04108 
04110 
04111     if( (phi_init1 != NULL) && (phi_init2 != NULL) )
04112     {
04113         memcpy(phi_init1,phi_init2,img_size);
04114     }
04115     clean_boundaries(phi_init2,phi_init2_clean);
04116     if( (phi_init1_clean != NULL) && (phi_init2_clean != NULL) )
04117     {
04118         memcpy(phi_init1_clean,phi_init2_clean,img_size);
04119     }
04120     phiInit2imgPhi();
04121 
04122     QSettings settings;
04123 
04124     settings.setValue("Settings/Algorithm/Na", Na1);
04125     settings.setValue("Settings/Algorithm/Ns", Ns1);
04126     settings.setValue("Settings/Algorithm/model", model);
04127     settings.setValue("Settings/Algorithm/isRgb", isRgb1);

04662 
04663 void ImageViewer::default_settings()
04664 {
04666 
04667     // paramètres par défaut de l'onglet Algorithm
04668 
04670 
04671     Na1 = 30;
04672     Ns1 = 3;
04673     model = 1;
04674     lambda_out1 = 1;
04675     lambda_in1 = 1;
04676     kernel_gradient_length1 = 5;
04677     alpha1 = 1;
04678     beta1 = 10;
04679     gamma1 = 10;
04680     hasSmoothingCycle1 = true;
04681     kernel_curve1 = 5;
04682     std_curve1 = 2.0;
04683     hasCleaning1 = true;
04684 
04686 
04688 
04689     // paramètres par défaut de l'onglet Initialisation
04690 
04692 
04693     hasEllipse1 = false;
04694     init_width1 = 0.95;
04695     init_height1 = 0.95;
04696     center_x1 = 0.0;
04697     center_y1 = 0.0;
04698 
04700 
04702 
04703     // paramètres par défaut de l'onglet Preprocessing
04704 
04706 
04707     hasPreprocess = false;
04708     hasGaussianNoise = false;
04709     std_noise = 20.0;

04753     Rout1 = 0;

04755     Bout1 = 255;
04756     Rin1 = 255;
04757     Gin1 = 0;

04775     cancel_settings();
04776

04778 
04779     QImage img_phi0 = QImage(100,100, QImage::Format_RGB888);
04780 
04781

04783

04785     {
04786         // i = x+y*img_width so
04787         y = i/100;
04788         x = i-y*100;
04789 
04790         if( x < 95 && x > 5 && y < 95 && y > 5 )
04791         {
04792             img_phi0.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(255,255,255));
04793         }
04794         else
04795         {
04796             img_phi0.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(0,0,0));
04797         }
04798     }
04799 
04800     img_phi = img_phi0.scaled( img_width, img_height, Qt::IgnoreAspectRatio, Qt::SmoothTransformation);
04801 
04802     imgPhi2phiInit();
04803 
04804     // pour afficher l'image dans la fenetre settings
04805     int n_out = 0;
04806     int n_in = 0;
04807     for( int i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
04808     {
04809         if( phi_init1_clean[i] == 1 )
04810         {
04811             Lout_2[n_out++] = i;
04812         }
04813         if( phi_init1_clean[i] == -1 )
04814         {
04815             Lin_2[n_in++] = i;
04816         }
04817     }
04818     Lout_2[n_out] = list_end;
04819     Lin_2[n_in] = list_end;
04820 
04821     filtering_visu();
04822     tab_visu(onglets->currentIndex());
04823 }

04836 // Nettoyage des frontières
04837 inline void ImageViewer::clean_boundaries(char* phi, char* phi_clean)
04838 {
04839     if( phi != NULL && phi_clean != NULL )
04840     {
04841         int i, x, y; // offset and position
04842 
04843         for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
04844         {
04845             if( phi[i] == 1 )
04846             {
04847                 // i = x+y*img_width so
04848                 y = i/img_width;
04849                 x = i-y*img_width;
04850 
04851                 // nettoyage si la condition de voisinage aux frontières n'est pas respectée
04852                 if( isRedundantPointOfLout(phi,x,y) )
04853                 {
04854                     phi_clean[i] = 3;
04855                 }
04856                 else
04857                 {
04858                     phi_clean[i] = 1;
04859                 }
04860             }
04861 
04862             if( phi[i] == -1 )
04863             {
04864                 // i = x+y*img_width so
04865                 y = i/img_width;
04866                 x = i-y*img_width;
04867 
04868                 if( isRedundantPointOfLin(phi,x,y) )
04869                 {
04870                     phi_clean[i] = -3;
04871                 }
04872                 else
04873                 {
04874                     phi_clean[i] = -1;
04875                 }
04876             }
04877         }
04878 
04879         // efface l'affichage des listes
04880         for( int n_out = 0; Lout_2[n_out] != list_end; n_out++ )
04881         {
04882             i = Lout_2[n_out]*3;
04883 
04884             image_phi_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04885             image_phi_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04886             image_phi_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04887 
04888             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04889             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04890             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04891         }
04892 
04893         for( int n_in = 0; Lin_2[n_in] != list_end; n_in++ )
04894         {
04895             i = Lin_2[n_in]*3;
04896 
04897             image_phi_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04898             image_phi_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04899             image_phi_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04900 
04901             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04902             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04903             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04904         }
04905 
04906         int n_out = 0;
04907         int n_in = 0;
04908         for( int i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
04909         {
04910             if( phi_clean[i] == 1 )
04911             {
04912                 Lout_2[n_out++] = i;
04913             }
04914             if( phi_clean[i] == -1 )
04915             {
04916                 Lin_2[n_in++] = i;
04917             }
04918         }
04919         Lout_2[n_out] = list_end;
04920         Lin_2[n_in] = list_end;
04921 
04922     }
04923     return;
04924 }
04925 
04926 inline bool ImageViewer::isRedundantPointOfLin(char* phi, int x, int y)
04927 {
04928     // if ∃ a neighbor ∈ Lout | ∈ Rout
04929 
04930     if( y-1 >= 0 )
04931     {
04932         if( phi[ x+(y-1)*img_width ] >= 0 )
04933         {
04934             return false; // is not redundant point of Lin
04935         }
04936     }
04937     if( x-1 >= 0 )
04938     {
04939         if( phi[ (x-1)+y*img_width ] >= 0 )
04940         {
04941             return false; // is not redundant point of Lin
04942         }
04943     }
04944     if( x+1 < img_width )
04945     {
04946         if( phi[ (x+1)+y*img_width ] >= 0 )
04947         {
04948             return false; // is not redundant point of Lin
04949         }
04950     }
04951     if( y+1 < img_height )
04952     {
04953         if( phi[ x+(y+1)*img_width ] >= 0 )
04954         {
04955             return false; // is not redundant point of Lin
04956         }
04957     }
04958 
04959     // ==> ∀ neighbors ∈ Lin | ∈ Rin
04960     return true; // is redundant point of Lin
04961 }
04962 
04963 // Fonction créee pour utiliser plusieurs return et sortir le plus tÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â´t possible quand le test est faux
04964 // permet contrairement à l'instruction break de sortir de toutes les sous-boucles d'un coup
04965 inline bool ImageViewer::isRedundantPointOfLout(char* phi, int x, int y)
04966 {
04967     // if ∃ a neighbor ∈ Lin | ∈ Rin
04968 
04969     if( y-1 >= 0 )
04970     {
04971         if( phi[ x+(y-1)*img_width ] <= 0 )
04972         {
04973             return false; // is not redundant point of Lout
04974         }
04975     }
04976     if( x-1 >= 0 )
04977     {
04978         if( phi[ (x-1)+y*img_width ] <= 0 )
04979         {
04980             return false; // is not redundant point of Lout
04981         }
04982     }
04983     if( x+1 < img_width )
04984     {
04985         if( phi[ (x+1)+y*img_width ] <= 0 )
04986         {
04987             return false; // is not redundant point of Lout
04988         }
04989     }
04990     if( y+1 < img_height )
04991     {
04992         if( phi[ x+(y+1)*img_width ] <= 0 )
04993         {
04994             return false; // is not redundant point of Lout
04995         }
04996     }
04997 
04998     // ==> ∀ neighbors ∈ Lout | ∈ Rout
04999     return true; // is redundant point of Lout
05000 }
05001 
05002 // Fonction appelée dans l'onglet initalisation pour calculer et afficher l'image+phi(couleur foncé)+forme(couleur clair)
05003 void ImageViewer::shape_visu()
05004 {
05005     if( shape != NULL )
05006     {
05007         init_width2 = double(width_shape_spin->value())/100.0;
05008         init_height2 = double(height_shape_spin->value())/100.0;
05009         center_x2 = double(abscissa_spin->value())/100.0;
05010         center_y2 = double(ordinate_spin->value())/100.0;
05011 
05012         if( rectangle_radio->isChecked() )
05013         {
05014             hasEllipse2 = false;
05015         }
05016         if( ellipse_radio->isChecked() )
05017         {
05018             hasEllipse2 = true;
05019         }
05020 
05021 
05022         int i, x, y; // offset and position
05023 
05024         // efface les listes de la QImage
05025         for( int n_out = 0; Lout_shape1[n_out] != list_end; n_out++ )
05026         {
05027             i = Lout_shape1[n_out]*3;
05028 
05029             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_phi_uchar[i];
05030             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_phi_uchar[i+1];
05031             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_phi_uchar[i+2];
05032         }
05033 
05034         for( int n_in = 0; Lin_shape1[n_in] != list_end; n_in++ )
05035         {
05036             i = Lin_shape1[n_in]*3;
05037 
05038             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_phi_uchar[i];
05039             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_phi_uchar[i+1];
05040             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_phi_uchar[i+2];
05041         }
05042 
05043         if( hasEllipse2 )
05044         {
05045             // Thanks to Alois Zingl for his ellipse Bresenham's Algorithm implementation
05046             // http://free.pages.at/easyfilter/bresenham.html
05047 
05048             int n = 0;
05049             int x0 = int((1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0 + center_x2*double(img_width));
05050             int y0 = int((1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0 + center_y2*double(img_height));
05051             int x1 = int((double(img_width)-(1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0) + center_x2*double(img_width));
05052             int y1 = int((double(img_height)-(1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0)+ center_y2*double(img_height));
05053 
05054             // values of diameter
05055             double a = abs(x1-x0);
05056             int b = abs(y1-y0);
05057 
05058             double b1 = b&1;
05059             double dx = double(4*(1-a)*b*b);
05060             double dy = double(4*(b1+1)*a*a);
05061             double err = dx+dy+double(b1*a*a); // error increment
05062             double e2; // error of 1.step
05063 
05064             if( x0 > x1 )
05065             {
05066                 x0 = x1; // if called with swapped points
05067                 x1 += int(a);
05068             }
05069 
05070             if( y0 > y1 )
05071             {
05072                 y0 = y1; // .. exchange them
05073             }
05074 
05075             y0 += (b+1)/2;
05076             y1 = y0-int(b1); // starting pixel
05077             a *= 8.0*a;
05078             b1 = 8.0*double(b)*double(b);
05079 
05080             do
05081             {
05082                 if( n < 2*img_size-20 )
05083                 {
05084                     for( int ddy = -2; ddy <= 2; ddy++ )
05085                     {
05086                         for( int ddx = -2; ddx <= 2; ddx++ )
05087                         {
05088                             shape_points[n++] = x1+ddx+(y0+ddy)*img_width; //   I. Quadrant
05089                             shape_points[n++] = x0+ddx+(y0+ddy)*img_width; //  II. Quadrant
05090                             shape_points[n++] = x0+ddx+(y1+ddy)*img_width; // III. Quadrant
05091                             shape_points[n++] = x1+ddx+(y1+ddy)*img_width; //  IV. Quadrant
05092                         }
05093                     }
05094                 }
05095 
05096                 e2 = 2.0*err;
05097 
05098                 // x step
05099                 if( e2 >= dx )
05100                 {
05101                     x0++;
05102                     x1--;
05103                     dx += b1;
05104                     err += dx;
05105                 }
05106 
05107                 // y step
05108                 if( e2 <= dy )
05109                 {
05110                     y0++;
05111                     y1--;
05112                     dy += a;
05113                     err += dy;
05114                 }
05115 
05116             }
05117             while( x0 <= x1 );
05118 
05119             // too early stop of flat ellipses a = 1
05120             // -> finish tip of ellipse
05121             while( y0-y1 < b )
05122             {
05123                 if( n < 2*img_size-20 )
05124                 {
05125                     for( int ddy = -2; ddy <= 2; ddy++ )
05126                     {
05127                         for( int ddx = -2; ddx <= 2; ddx++ )
05128                         {
05129                             shape_points[n++] = x0-1+ddx+(y0+ddy)*img_width;
05130                             shape_points[n++] = x1+1+ddx+(y0+ddy)*img_width;
05131                             shape_points[n++] = x0-1+ddx+(y1+ddy)*img_width;
05132                             shape_points[n++] = x1+1+ddx+(y1+ddy)*img_width;
05133                         }
05134                     }
05135                     y0++;
05136                     y1--;
05137                 }
05138             }
05139 
05140             // to mark the end;
05141             shape_points[n] = list_end;
05142 
05143             int n_out = 0;
05144             int n_in = 0;
05145             for( int n = 0; shape_points[n] != list_end; n++ )
05146             {
05147                 i = shape_points[n];
05148 
05149                 y = i/img_width;
05150                 x = i-y*img_width;
05151 
05152                 if( x >= 0 && x < img_width && y >= 0 && y < img_height )
05153                 {
05154                     if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05155                     {
05156                         if( (double(y-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) <= 1.0 )
05157                         {
05158                             if( Lout_shape1[n_out] != i )
05159                             {
05160                                 Lout_shape1[n_out++] = i;
05161                             }
05162                         }
05163 
05164                         if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) <= 1.0 )
05165                         {
05166                             if( Lout_shape1[n_out] != i )
05167                             {
05168                                 Lout_shape1[n_out++] = i;
05169                             }
05170                         }
05171 
05172                         if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) <= 1.0 )
05173                         {
05174                             if( Lout_shape1[n_out] != i )
05175                             {
05176                                 Lout_shape1[n_out++] = i;
05177                             }
05178                         }
05179 
05180                         if( (double(y+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) <= 1.0 )
05181                         {
05182                             if( Lout_shape1[n_out] != i )
05183                             {
05184                                 Lout_shape1[n_out++] = i;
05185                             }
05186                         }
05187                     }
05188                     else
05189                     {
05190                         if( (double(y-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05191                         {
05192                             if( Lin_shape1[n_in] != i )
05193                             {
05194                                 Lin_shape1[n_in++] = i;
05195                             }
05196                         }
05197 
05198                         if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x-1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05199                         {
05200                             if( Lin_shape1[n_in] != i )
05201                             {
05202                                 Lin_shape1[n_in++] = i;
05203                             }
05204                         }
05205 
05206                         if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05207                         {
05208                             if( Lin_shape1[n_in] != i )
05209                             {
05210                                 Lin_shape1[n_in++] = i;
05211                             }
05212                         }
05213 
05214                         if( (double(y+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y+1)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05215                         {
05216                             if( Lin_shape1[n_in] != i )
05217                             {
05218                                 Lin_shape1[n_in++] = i;
05219                             }
05220                         }
05221                     }
05222                 }
05223 
05224             }
05225 
05226             Lout_shape1[n_out] = list_end;
05227             Lin_shape1[n_in] = list_end;
05228         }
05229         else
05230         {
05231             int x1, y1;
05232 
05233             int n = 0;
05234             for( x = int((1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0 + center_x2*double(img_width)); x < int((double(img_width)-(1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0) + center_x2*double(img_width)); x++ )
05235             {
05236                 y = int((1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0 + center_y2*double(img_height));
05237                 y1 = int((double(img_height)-(1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0)+ center_y2*double(img_height));
05238 
05239                 if( n < 2*img_size-10 )
05240                 {
05241                     for( int dy = -2; dy <= 2; dy++ )
05242                     {
05243                         for( int dx = -2; dx <= 2; dx++ )
05244                         {
05245                             shape_points[n++] = x+dx+(y+dy)*img_width;
05246                             shape_points[n++] = x+dx+(y1+dy)*img_width;
05247                         }
05248                     }
05249                 }
05250             }
05251

05425 // Remet phi_init2_clean a zéro, c'est à dire tout correspond à l'extérieur
05426 void ImageViewer::clean_phi_visu()
05427 {
05428     if( phi_init2 != NULL && phi_init2_clean != NULL )
05429     {
05430         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
05431         for( int i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05432         {
05433             phi_init2[i] = 1;
05434             phi_init2_clean[i] = 3;
05435         }
05436         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
05437 
05438         shape_visu();
05439 
05440     }
05441 }
05442 
05443 // Soustrait une forme à phi_init2
05444 void ImageViewer::phi_subtract_shape()
05445 {
05446     if( shape != NULL && phi_init2 != NULL )
05447     {
05448 
05449         int i, x, y;
05450 
05451         if( hasEllipse2 )
05452         {
05453             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05454             {
05455                 y = i/img_width;
05456                 x = i-y*img_width;
05457 
05458                 // inéquation de l'ellipse
05459                 // grand axe et petit axe proportionnel à la largeur et la hauteur de l'image
05460                 // pour une image carrée, l'ellipse est un cercle
05461                 // variable init_shape_size par défaut a 0.95 (entre 0 et 1 sinon)
05462                 if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05463                 {
05464                     shape[i] = 1;
05465                 }
05466                 else
05467                 {
05468                     shape[i] = -1;
05469                 }
05470             }
05471 
05472         }
05473 
05474         else
05475         {
05476             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05477             {
05478                 y = i/img_width;
05479                 x = i-y*img_width;
05480 
05481                 // pour faire un rectangle
05482                 // largeur et hauteur du rectangle proportionnel à la largeur et la hauteur de l'image
05483                 // pour une image carrée, le rectangle est un carré
05484                 if( double(y) > ((1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0 + center_y2*double(img_height)) && double(y) < ((double(img_height)-(1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0) + center_y2*double(img_height)) && double(x) > ((1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0 + center_x2*double(img_width)) && double(x) < ((double(img_width)-(1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0) + center_x2*double(img_width)) )
05485                 {
05486                     shape[i] = -1;
05487                 }
05488                 else
05489                 {
05490                     shape[i] = 1;
05491                 }
05492             }
05493 
05494         }
05495 
05496         bool phi_init2_modif = false;
05497 
05498         for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05499         {
05500             if( shape[i] == -1 && phi_init2[i] == -1 )
05501             {
05502                 phi_init2[i] = 1;
05503                 phi_init2_modif = true;
05504             }
05505         }
05506 
05507         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
05508 
05509         if( !phi_init2_modif )
05510         {
05511             bool hasOne = false;
05512             bool hasMinusOne = false;
05513 
05514             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05515             {
05516                 if( shape[i] == 1 )
05517                 {
05518                     hasOne = true;
05519                 }
05520                 if( shape[i] == -1 )
05521                 {
05522                     hasMinusOne = true;
05523                 }
05524             }
05525 
05526             if( hasOne && hasMinusOne )
05527             {
05528                 phi_add_shape();
05529             }
05530         }
05531     }
05532 
05533     return;
05534 }
05535 
05536 // Ajoute une forme à phi_init2
05537 void ImageViewer::phi_add_shape()
05538 {
05539     if( shape != NULL && phi_init2 != NULL )
05540     {
05541         int i, x, y;
05542 
05543         if( hasEllipse2 )
05544         {
05545             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05546             {
05547                 y = i/img_width;
05548                 x = i-y*img_width;
05549 
05550                 // inéquation de l'ellipse
05551                 // grand axe et petit axe proportionnel à la largeur et la hauteur de l'image
05552                 // pour une image carrée, l'ellipse est un cercle
05553                 // variable init_shape_size par défaut a 0.95 (entre 0 et 1 sinon)
05554                 if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 )
05555                 {
05556                     shape[i] = 1;
05557                 }
05558                 else
05559                 {
05560                     shape[i] = -1;
05561                 }
05562             }
05563         }
05564 
05565         else
05566         {
05567             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05568             {
05569                 y = i/img_width;
05570                 x = i-y*img_width;
05571 
05572                 // pour faire un rectangle
05573                 // largeur et hauteur du rectangle proportionnel à la largeur et la hauteur de l'image
05574                 // pour une image carrée, le rectangle est un carré
05575                 if( double(y) > ((1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0 + center_y2*double(img_height)) && double(y) < ((double(img_height)-(1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0) + center_y2*double(img_height)) && double(x) > ((1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0 + center_x2*double(img_width)) && double(x) < ((double(img_width)-(1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0) + center_x2*double(img_width)) )
05576                 {
05577                     shape[i] = -1;
05578                 }
05579                 else
05580                 {
05581                     shape[i] = 1;
05582                 }
05583             }
05584         }
05585 
05586         bool phi_init2_modif = false;
05587 
05588         for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05589         {
05590             if( shape[i] == -1 && phi_init2[i] == 1 )
05591             {
05592                 phi_init2[i] = -1;
05593                 phi_init2_modif = true;
05594             }
05595         }
05596 
05597         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
05598 
05599         if( !phi_init2_modif )
05600         {
05601             bool hasOne = false;
05602             bool hasMinusOne = false;
05603 
05604             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
05605             {
05606                 if( shape[i] == 1 )
05607                 {
05608                     hasOne = true;
05609                 }
05610                 if( shape[i] == -1 )
05611                 {
05612                     hasMinusOne = true;
05613                 }
05614             }
05615 
05616             if( hasOne && hasMinusOne )
05617             {
05618                 phi_subtract_shape();
05619             }
05620         }
05621     }
05622 
05623     return;
05624 }

05765                 image_phi_uchar[i] = Rin2/2;
05766                 image_phi_uchar[i+1] = Gin2/2;
05767                 image_phi_uchar[i+2] = Bin2/2;
05768 
05769                 image_shape_uchar[i] = Rin2/2;
05770                 image_shape_uchar[i+1] = Gin2/2;
05771                 image_shape_uchar[i+2] = Bin2/2;
05772             }
05773         }
05774 
05775 
05776         else
05777         {
05778             for( int n_out = 0; Lout_2[n_out] != list_end; n_out++ )
05779             {
05780                 i = Lout_2[n_out]*3;
05781 
05782                 image_phi_uchar[i] = Rout2;
05783                 image_phi_uchar[i+1] = Gout2;
05784                 image_phi_uchar[i+2] = Bout2;
05785 
05786                 image_shape_uchar[i] = Rout2/2;
05787                 image_shape_uchar[i+1] = Gout2/2;
05788                 image_shape_uchar[i+2] = Bout2/2;
05789             }
05790 
05791             for( int n_in = 0; Lin_2[n_in] != list_end; n_in++ )
05792             {
05793                 i = Lin_2[n_in]*3;
05794 
05795                 image_phi_uchar[i] = Rin2;
05796                 image_phi_uchar[i+1] = Gin2;
05797                 image_phi_uchar[i+2] = Bin2;
05798 
05799                 image_shape_uchar[i] = Rin2/2;
05800                 image_shape_uchar[i+1] = Gin2/2;
05801                 image_shape_uchar[i+2] = Bin2/2;
05802             }
05803         }
05804 
05805         if( hasContoursHidden && onglets->currentIndex() == 2 )
05806         {
05807             // affiche l'ellipse ou le rectangle
05808             imageLabel_settings->set_qimage(image_filter);
05809         }
05810         else
05811         {
05812            // affiche l'ellipse ou le rectangle
05813            imageLabel_settings->set_qimage(image_phi);
05814         }
05815 
05816         // efface l'ellipse ou le recangle de la QImage
05817         // efface les listes de la QImage
05818         for( int n_out = 0; Lout_shape1[n_out] != list_end; n_out++ )
05819         {
05820             i = Lout_shape1[n_out]*3;
05821 
05822             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_phi_uchar[i];
05823             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_phi_uchar[i+1];
05824             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_phi_uchar[i+2];
05825         }
05826 
05827         for( int n_in = 0; Lin_shape1[n_in] != list_end; n_in++ )
05828         {
05829             i = Lin_shape1[n_in]*3;
05830 
05831             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_phi_uchar[i];
05832             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_phi_uchar[i+1];
05833             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_phi_uchar[i+2];
05834         }
05835     }
05836 
05837     return;
05838 
05839 
05840 }

05872 // Fonction appelée quand on clique sur save
05873 void ImageViewer::saveImage()
05874 {
05875     QFileInfo fi(fileName);
05876     QString fileName_save;
05877 
05878     // selection du chemin à partir d'une boÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â®te de dialogue
05879     if( iterations1 == -1 )
05880     {
05881         fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05882                                                      tr("Save the image displayed by the main window"),
05883                                                      last_directory_used + "/" + fi.baseName(),
05884                                                      "PNG (*.png)");
05885     }
05886     else
05887     {
05888         if( image_disp == 1 )
05889         {
05890             fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05891                                                          tr("Save the image displayed by the main window"),
05892                                                          last_directory_used + "/" + fi.baseName()+tr("_with_phi(t=")+QString::number(iterations1)+")",
05893                                                          "PNG (*.png)");
05894         }
05895         if( image_disp == 2 && (hasPreprocess || model == 2) )
05896         {
05897             fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05898                                                          tr("Save the image displayed by the main window"),
05899                                                          last_directory_used + "/" + tr("preprocessed_") +fi.baseName()+tr("_with_phi(t=")+QString::number(iterations1)+")",
05900                                                          "PNG (*.png)");
05901 
05902         }
05903 
05904     }
05905 
05906     // sauvegarde
05907     QImage img_displayed=imageLabel->get_qimage();
05908     img_displayed.save(fileName_save);
05909 
05910     if( (hasPreprocess || model == 2) && !image_save_preprocess.isNull() )
05911     {
05912         // sélection du chemin+nom de sauvegarde à partir d'une boÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â®te de dialogue
05913         QString fileName_save2 = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05914                                                               tr("Save the preprocessed image"),
05915                                                               last_directory_used + "/" + tr("preprocessed_") + fi.baseName() + ".png",
05916                                                               "PNG (*.png)");
05917 
05918         // sauvegarde
05919         image_save_preprocess.save(fileName_save2);
05920 
05921     }
05922 
05923 }

05925 // Fonction appelée par le boutton selected de boundaries outside
05926 // sélection et affichage d'une couleur particulière
05927 void ImageViewer::color_out()
05928 {
05929     // Sélection d'une QColor a partir d'une boite de dialogue couleur
05930     QColor color_out = QColorDialog::getColor(Qt::white, this, tr("Select Lout color"));
05931     if( color_out.isValid() )
05932     {
05933         Rout_selected2 = (unsigned char)(color_out.red());
05934         Gout_selected2 = (unsigned char)(color_out.green());
05935         Bout_selected2 = (unsigned char)(color_out.blue());
05936 
05937         QPixmap pm(12,12);
05938         pm.fill(color_out);
05939         outsidecolor_combobox->addItem (pm, tr("Selected"));
05940         outsidecolor_combobox->removeItem (8);
05941 
05942         outsidecolor_combobox->setCurrentIndex(8);
05943     }
05944     // affichage de l'image avec la nouvelle couleur sélectionnée
05945     phi_visu(false);
05946 
05947 }

06136

06139         gamma2 = Vspin->value();
06140

06144         }
06145         else

06170

06257                         }

06260

06474                         }
06475                     }
06476 
06477                     for( int i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
06478                     {
06479                         I = (unsigned char)(255.0*double(img1_filtered[i]-min)/double(max-min));
06480 
06481                         image_filter_uchar[3*i] = I;
06482                         image_filter_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
06483                         image_filter_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
06484 
06485                         image_phi_uchar[3*i] = I;
06486                         image_phi_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
06487                         image_phi_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
06488 
06489                         image_shape_uchar[3*i] = I;
06490                         image_shape_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
06491                         image_shape_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
06492                     }
06493 
06494                 }
06495 
06496                 else
06497                 {
06498                     for( int i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
06499                     {
06500                         I = img1_filtered[i];
06501 
06502                         image_filter_uchar[3*i] = I;
06503                         image_filter_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
06504                         image_filter_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
06505 
06506                         image_phi_uchar[3*i] = I;
06507                         image_phi_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
06508                         image_phi_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
06509 
06510                         image_shape_uchar[3*i] = I;
06511                         image_shape_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
06512                         image_shape_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
06513                     }
06514 
06515                 }
06516             }
06517         }
06518 
06519         phi_visu(false);
06520     }
06521     return;
06522 }
06523

06533 // Fonction appelée à chaque changement d'onglet
06534 void ImageViewer::tab_visu(int value)
06535 {
06536     if( img1 != NULL )
06537     {
06538         // si onglet initilisation
06539         if( value == 1 )
06540         {
06541             imageLabel_settings->set_doWheelEvent(false);

06544             shape_visu();
06545         }
06546         else
06547         {
06548             imageLabel_settings->set_doWheelEvent(true);

06550             phi_visu(false); 
06551         }
06552     }
06553 }

06555 // Evénement clic souris dans imageLabel (image de la fenêtre principale) permet de rentrer dans la boucle infinie ou d'en sortir pour bloquer momentanément l'algo et prendre du temps sur une étape du contour actif
06556 void ImageViewer::mousePressEvent(QMouseEvent *event)
06557 {
06558     // si l'image est chargée
06559     if( img1 != NULL )
06560     {
06561         if( !startAct->isEnabled() )
06562         {
06563             if( event->button() == Qt::LeftButton )
06564             {
06565                 hasStepByStep = false;
06566                 hasClickStopping = true;
06567             }
06568 
06569             if( event->button() == Qt::RightButton )
06570             {
06571                 hasClickStopping = false;
06572                 hasStepByStep = true;
06573             }
06574 
06575         }
06576 
06577         else
06578         {
06579             if( event->button() == Qt::RightButton )
06580             {
06581                 hasStepByStep = true;
06582                 start();
06583             }
06584         }
06585     }
06586 }

06616 // Evénement touche clavier enfoncé dans imageLabel (image de la fenêtre principale) permet de rentrer dans la boucle infinie ou d'en sortir pour bloquer momentanément l'algo et prendre du temps sur une étape du contour actif
06617 void ImageViewer::keyPressEvent(QKeyEvent *event)

06623         {

06627                 {
06628                     hasStepByStep = false;
06629                     hasClickStopping = true;
06630                 }
06631             }

06634             {
06635                 hasClickStopping = false;
06636                 hasStepByStep = true;
06637             }
06638 
06639         }
06640 
06641         else
06642         {
06643             if( !event->isAutoRepeat() )
06644             {
06645                 if( event->key() == Qt::Key_Return || event->key() == Qt::Key_Up || event->key() == Qt::Key_Down )
06646                 {
06647                     hasClickStopping = false;
06648                     hasStepByStep = true;
06649                     start();
06650                 }
06651             }
06652 
06653         }
06654     }

06685 // Boucle infinie dont on peut rentrer ou sortir par un clic gauche ou droite (sur imageLabel, image de la fenêtre principale) lors de l'execution de l'algorithme et permettant de voir une étape particulière ou chaque étape, au rythme voulue
06686 void ImageViewer::infinite_loop()
06687 {
06688     while( hasClickStopping )
06689     {
06690         QApplication::processEvents();
06691     }

06694 // Evénement déplacement souris au niveau de imageLabel pour pouvoir donner les infos pixels
06695 void ImageViewer::mouseMoveEvent(QMouseEvent *event)
06696 {
06697     // si l'image est chargée
06698     if( img1 != NULL )
06699     {
06700         positionX = int(double(img_width)*double(   (  (event->pos()).x() -imageLabel->get_xoffset()    ) /double(imageLabel->getPixWidth())));
06701         positionY = int(double(img_height)*double(   (  (event->pos()).y() -imageLabel->get_yoffset()   ) /double(imageLabel->getPixHeight())));
06702 
06703         if( positionX >= 0 && positionX < img_width && positionY >= 0 && positionY < img_height )
06704         {
06705             if( image_disp == 1 )
06706             {
06707                 if( !isRgb1 )
06708                 {
06709                     int I = img1[ positionX+positionY*img_width ];
06710                     QColor RGB(I,I,I);
06711                     pixel_text->setText(tr("img(")+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+QString::number(I));
06712 
06713                 }
06714                 else
06715                 {
06716                     QColor RGB(img1[ 3*(positionX+positionY*img_width) ], img1[ 3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+1 ], img1[ 3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+2 ]);
06717                     pixel_text->setText(tr("img(")+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(img1[ 3*(positionX+positionY*img_width) ])+","+QString::number(img1[ 3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+1 ])+","+QString::number(img1[ 3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+2 ])+")");
06718                 }
06719 
06720             }
06721 
06722             if( image_disp == 2 )
06723             {
06724                 const unsigned char* img1_filtered;
06725 
06726                 QString img_str;
06727                 if( !hasPreprocess )
06728                 {
06729                     img_str = tr("img(");
06730                 }
06731                 else
06732                 {
06733                     img_str = tr("img'(");
06734                 }
06735 
06736                 if( !isRgb1 )
06737                 {
06738                     img1_filtered = filters1->get_filtered();
06739                     int I = img1_filtered[positionX+positionY*img_width];
06740                     QColor RGB(I,I,I);
06741                     pixel_text->setText(img_str+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+QString::number(I));
06742                 }
06743 
06744                 else
06745                 {
06746                     if( model == 1 )
06747                     {
06748                         img1_filtered = filtersRGB1->get_filtered();
06749 
06750                         QColor RGB(img1_filtered[3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)],img1_filtered[3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+1],img1_filtered[3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+2]);
06751 
06752                         pixel_text->setText(img_str+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(img1_filtered[3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)])+","+QString::number(img1_filtered[3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+1])+","+QString::number(img1_filtered[3*(positionX+positionY*img_width)+2])+")");
06753 
06754                     }
06755                     if( model == 2 )
06756                     {
06757                         img1_filtered = filtersRGB1->get_gradient();
06758 
06759                         int I = img1_filtered[ positionX+positionY*img_width ];
06760                         QColor RGB(I,I,I);
06761                         pixel_text->setText(img_str+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+QString::number(I));
06762 
06763                     }
06764 
06765                 }
06766             }
06767             show_phi_list_value();
06768         }
06769     }
06770 
06771 }
06772 
06773 inline void ImageViewer::show_phi_list_value()
06774 {
06775     const char* phi = NULL;
06776 
06777     if( !isRgb1 )
06778     {
06779         if( model == 1 )
06780         {
06781             if( acWithoutEdges1 != NULL )
06782             {
06783                 phi = acWithoutEdges1->get_phi();
06784             }
06785         }
06786 
06787         if( model == 2 )
06788         {
06789             if( geodesicAc1 != NULL )
06790             {
06791                 phi = geodesicAc1->get_phi();
06792             }
06793         }
06794 
06795     }
06796 
06797     else
06798     {
06799         if( model == 1 )
06800         {
06801             if( acWithoutEdgesYUV1 != NULL )
06802             {
06803                 phi = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_phi();
06804             }
06805         }
06806 
06807         if( model == 2 )
06808         {
06809             if( geodesicAc1 != NULL )
06810             {
06811                 phi = geodesicAc1->get_phi();
06812             }
06813         }
06814     }
06815 
06816     if( phi != NULL )
06817     {
06818         QColor RGBout(Rout1,Gout1,Bout1);
06819         QColor RGBin(Rin1,Gin1,Bin1);
06820 
06821         if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == 3 )
06822         {
06823             phi_text->setText("ϕ("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06824             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ∉ "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"Lout"+"<font color=black>"+" & ∉ "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"Lin");
06825         }
06826         else if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == -3 )
06827         {
06828             phi_text->setText("ϕ("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06829             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ∉ "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"Lin"+"<font color=black>"+" & ∉ "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"Lout");
06830         }
06831 
06832         else if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == 1 )
06833         {
06834             phi_text->setText("ϕ("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06835             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ∈ "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"Lout");
06836         }
06837         else if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == -1 )
06838         {
06839             phi_text->setText("ϕ("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06840             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ∈ "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"Lin");
06841         }
06842     }
06843 
06844 }

06846 // Pour arrêter manuellement l'algorithme, s'il y a un problème au niveau des conditions d'arrêts ou du temps de calcul sur les grandes images
06847 void ImageViewer::stop()
06848 {
06849     hasClickStopping = false;
06850     hasAlgoBreaking = true;
06851 }
