06853 // Filtre des événements pour avoir le tracking au niveau du widget image de la fenêtre principale et de la fenêtre de parametres et pour ne pas avoir le tracking/la position au niveau de l'ensemble de chaque fenêtre
06854 bool ImageViewer::eventFilter(QObject *object, QEvent *event)
06855 {
06856     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabel et pas main_window
06857     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove )
06858     {
06859         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06860         mouseMoveEvent(mouseEvent);
06861     }
06862 
06863     // pour avoir les evénements keyPress
06864     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::KeyPress )
06865     {
06866         QKeyEvent* keyEvent = static_cast<QKeyEvent*>(event);
06867         keyPressEvent(keyEvent);
06868     }
06869 
06870     // pour avoir les evénements keyRelease
06871     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::KeyRelease )
06872     {
06873         QKeyEvent* keyEvent = static_cast<QKeyEvent*>(event);
06874         keyReleaseEvent(keyEvent);
06875     }
06876 
06877     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel
06878     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
06879     {
06880         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06881         mousePressEvent(mouseEvent);
06882     }
06883 
06884     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel
06885     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonRelease )
06886     {
06887         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06888         mouseReleaseEvent(mouseEvent);
06889     }
06890 
06891     // molette prise en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel
06892     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && (img1 != NULL) )
06893     {
06894         imageLabel->set_hasText(false);
06895         imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06896         disconnect(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll (int,int)));
06897         disconnect(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll(int,int)));
06898         scale_spin0->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabel->get_zoomFactor()));
06899         connect(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll (int,int)));
06900         connect(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll(int,int)));
06901     }
06902 
06903     if( (object == scale_spin0 || object == scale_slider0 || object == scale_spin || object == scale_slider) && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
06904     {
06905         if( img1 != NULL )
06906         {
06907             imageLabel->set_hasText(false);
06908             imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06909             imageLabel_settings->set_hasText(false);
06910             imageLabel_settings->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06911         }
06912         positionX = img_width/2;
06913         positionY = img_height/2;
06914     }
06915 
06916 
06917     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabel_settings et pas settings_window
06918     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove )
06919     {
06920         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06921         mouseMoveEvent2(mouseEvent);
06922     }
06923 
06924     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel_settings
06925     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
06926     {
06927         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06928         mousePressEvent2(mouseEvent);
06929     }
06930 
06931     // molette prise en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel_settings
06932     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && (img1 != NULL) )
06933     {
06934         imageLabel_settings->set_hasText(false);
06935         imageLabel_settings->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06936         disconnect(scrollArea_settings->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll_settings(int,int)));
06937         disconnect(scrollArea_settings->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll_settings(int,int)));
06938         scale_spin->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabel_settings->get_zoomFactor()));
06939         connect(scrollArea_settings->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll_settings(int,int)));
06940         connect(scrollArea_settings->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll_settings(int,int)));
06941         QWheelEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QWheelEvent*>(event);
06942         wheelEvent(mouseEvent);
06943     }
06944 
06945     if( object == scale_spinA && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
06946     {
06947         if( !image1.isNull() )
06948         {
06949             imageLabelA->set_hasText(false);
06950             imageLabelA->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06951         }
06952         positionXa = imgA_width/2;
06953         positionYa = imgA_height/2;
06954     }
06955 
06956     if( object == scale_spinB && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
06957     {
06958         if( !image2.isNull() )
06959         {
06960             imageLabelB->set_hasText(false);
06961             imageLabelB->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06962         }
06963         positionXb = imgB_width/2;
06964         positionYb = imgB_height/2;
06965     }
06966 
06967     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabelA
06968     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove )
06969     {
06970         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06971         mouseMoveEventA(mouseEvent);
06972     }
06973     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabelA
06974     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
06975     {
06976         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06977         mousePressEventA(mouseEvent);
06978     }
06979 
06980     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && !image1.isNull() )
06981     {
06982         imageLabelA->set_hasText(false);
06983         imageLabelA->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06984         disconnect(scrollAreaA->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollA (int,int)));
06985         disconnect(scrollAreaA->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollA(int,int)));
06986         scale_spinA->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabelA->get_zoomFactor()));
06987         connect(scrollAreaA->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollA (int,int)));
06988         connect(scrollAreaA->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollA(int,int)));
06989     }
06990 
06991     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && !image2.isNull() )
06992     {
06993         imageLabelB->set_hasText(false);
06994         imageLabelB->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06995         disconnect(scrollAreaB->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollB (int,int)));
06996         disconnect(scrollAreaB->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollB(int,int)));
06997         scale_spinB->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabelB->get_zoomFactor()));
06998         connect(scrollAreaB->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollB (int,int)));
06999         connect(scrollAreaB->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollB(int,int)));
07000     }
07001 
07002     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabelB
07003     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove )
07004     {
07005         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
07006         mouseMoveEventB(mouseEvent);
07007     }
07008     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabelB
07009     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress )
07010     {
07011         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
07012         mousePressEventB(mouseEvent);
07013     }
07014 
07015 
07016     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter )
07017     {
07018         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
07019         dragEnterEvent(drag);
07020     }
07021     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove )
07022     {
07023         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
07024         dragMoveEvent(drag);
07025     }
07026     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::Drop )
07027     {
07028         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
07029         dropEvent(drag);
07030     }
07031     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave )
07032     {
07033         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
07034         dragLeaveEvent(drag);
07035     }
07036 
07037     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter )
07038     {
07039         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
07040         dragEnterEventPhi(drag);
07041     }
07042     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove )
07043     {
07044         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
07045         dragMoveEventPhi(drag);
07046     }
07047     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::Drop )
07048     {
07049         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
07050         dropEventPhi(drag);
07051     }
07052     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave )
07053     {
07054         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
07055         dragLeaveEventPhi(drag);
07056     }
07057 
07058     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter )
07059     {
07060         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
07061         dragEnterEventA(drag);
07062     }
07063     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove )
07064     {
07065         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
07066         dragMoveEventA(drag);
07067     }
07068     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::Drop )
07069     {
07070         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
07071         dropEventA(drag);
07072     }
07073     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave )
07074     {
07075         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
07076         dragLeaveEventA(drag);
07077     }
07078 
07079     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter )
07080     {
07081         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
07082         dragEnterEventB(drag);
07083     }
07084     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove )
07085     {
07086         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
07087         dragMoveEventB(drag);
07088     }
07089     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::Drop )
07090     {
07091         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
07092         dropEventB(drag);
07093     }
07094     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave )
07095     {
07096         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
07097         dragLeaveEventB(drag);
07098     }
07099 
07100     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove && positionX >= 0 && positionX < img_width && positionY >= 0 && positionY < img_height )
07101     {
07102         setCursor(Qt::CrossCursor);
07103     }
07104     else
07105     {
07106         setCursor(Qt::ArrowCursor);
07107     }
07108 
07109     return false;
07110 }
07111 
07112 // Evénement de déplacement de la souris dans le widget image de la fenêtre de paramètres
07113 void ImageViewer::mouseMoveEvent2(QMouseEvent *event2)
07114 {
07115     // si l'image est chargée et si on est dans l'onglet initialisation
07116     if( img1 != NULL )
07117     {
07118         // position de la souris dans l'image
07119         positionX = int(double(img_width)*double(   (  (event2->pos()).x() -imageLabel_settings->get_xoffset()   ) /double(imageLabel_settings->getPixWidth())));
07120         positionY = int(double(img_height)*double(   (  (event2->pos()).y() -imageLabel_settings->get_yoffset()   ) /double(imageLabel_settings->getPixHeight())));
07121 
07122         if( onglets->currentIndex() == 1 )
07123         {
07124             // on en deduit les valeurs relatives des sliders en %
07125 
07126             double a = (double(positionX)-double(img_width/2))/double(img_width);
07127             double b = (double(positionY)-double(img_height/2))/double(img_height);
07128 
07129             abscissa_spin->setValue(int(a*100.0));
07130             ordinate_spin->setValue(int(b*100.0));
07131         }
07132     }
07133 
07134 }
07135

07138 // Evénement clic souris dans le widget image de la fenêtre de paramètres
07139 void ImageViewer::mousePressEvent2(QMouseEvent *event2)
07140 {
07141     // si on est dans l'onglet d'initilisation
07142     if( (img1 != NULL) && onglets->currentIndex() == 1 )
07143     {
07144         // clic gauche, on ajoute une forme
07145         if( event2->button() == Qt::LeftButton )
07146         {
07147             add_visu();
07148         }
07149         // clic droit, on soustraie
07150         if( event2->button() == Qt::RightButton )
07151         {
07152             subtract_visu();
07153         }
07154         // clic du milieu, on change un rectangle en ellipse ou vice versa
07155         if( event2->button() == Qt::MidButton )
07156         {
07157             if( !rectangle_radio->isChecked() )
07158             {
07159                 rectangle_radio->setChecked(true);
07160             }
07161             else
07162             {
07163                 ellipse_radio->setChecked(true);
07164             }
07165             shape_visu();
07166         }
07167     }
07168 
07169     // pour cacher ou non au clic gauche le contour actif initial quand on est dans l'onglet Preprocessing
07170     if( (img1 != NULL) && onglets->currentIndex() == 2 )
07171     {
07172         if( event2->button() == Qt::RightButton )
07173         {
07174             if( hasContoursHidden )
07175             {
07176                 hasContoursHidden = false;
07177             }
07178             else
07179             {
07180                 hasContoursHidden = true;
07181             }
07182             phi_visu(false);
07183         }
07184         if( event2->button() == Qt::LeftButton )
07185         {
07186             hasContoursHidden = true;
07187             if( hasShowImg1 )
07188             {
07189                 hasShowImg1 = false;
07190                 img1_visu();
07191             }
07192             else
07193             {
07194                 hasShowImg1 = true;
07195                 phi_visu(false);
07196             }
07197         }
07198     }
07199 
07200  }

07203 void ImageViewer::img1_visu()

07207         imageLabel_settings->set_qimage(img);

07211 // Evénement de la molette de souris utilisé dans l'onglet Initialization pour agrandir ou rétrecir la forme
07212 void ImageViewer::wheelEvent(QWheelEvent *event)
07213 {
07214     // si une image est déja chargée et si on est dans l'onglet d'initialisation
07215     if( (img1 != NULL) && onglets->currentIndex() == 1 )
07216     {
07217         // nombre de degré et de pas de la molette
07218         int numDegrees = event->delta() / 8;
07219         int numSteps = numDegrees / 15;
07220 
07221         // récupération des valeurs des sliders concernant la taille de la forme
07222         int width_ratio = width_shape_spin->value();
07223         int height_ratio = height_shape_spin->value();
07224 
07225         // correpondance par rapport à la taille réelle de la forme
07226         double width = double(img_width)*double(width_ratio)/100.0;
07227         double height = double(img_height)*double(height_ratio)/100.0;
07228 
07229         // augmentation ou diminution de 15% à chaque pas de molette
07230         width += 0.15*double(numSteps)*width;
07231         height += 0.15*double(numSteps)*height;
07232 
07233         width_ratio = int( round(100.0*width/double(img_width)) );
07234         height_ratio = int( round(100.0*height/double(img_height)) );
07235 
07236         if( (width_ratio > 3) && (height_ratio > 3) && (width_ratio < 150) && (height_ratio < 150) )
07237         {
07238             width_shape_spin->setValue(width_ratio);
07239             height_shape_spin->setValue(height_ratio);
07240         }
07241 
07242         event->accept();
07243     }
07244 }
07245

07276 // Ouverture de l'image 1 appelée par le boutton 1 de la fenêtre d'évaluation
07277 void ImageViewer::open_imageA()
07278 {
07279     if( !fileNameA.isEmpty() )
07280     {
07281         image1 = QImage(fileNameA);
07282         if( image1.isNull() )
07283         {
07284             QMessageBox::information(this, tr("Opening error - Ofeli"),
07285                                      tr("Cannot load %1.").arg(fileNameA));
07286             return;
07287         }
07288 
07289         imageLabelA->set_qimage0(image1);
07290         QApplication::processEvents();
07291 
07292         imgA_height = image1.height();
07293         imgA_width = image1.width();
07294         imgA_size = imgA_width*imgA_height;
07295 
07296         positionXa = imgA_width/2;
07297         positionYa = imgA_height/2;
07298 
07299         QFileInfo fi1(fileNameA);
07300         QString name1 = fi1.fileName();
07301 
07302         QString string_lists_text;
07303         string_lists_text=QString::number(imgA_width)+"×"+QString::number(imgA_height);
07304         label_name1->setText(name1 +" - "+string_lists_text);
07305     }
07306 }

07455 // Fonction exécutée quand on appuye sur le boutton Compute de la fenêtre d'évaluation
07456 // calcule et affiche les distances d'Hausdorff et Hausdorff modifiée
07457 void ImageViewer::compute(int index)
07458 {
07459     if( index == 1 )
07460     {
07461         // les deux pointeurs doivent pointés sur un espace mémoire alloué
07462         if( !image1.isNull() && !image2.isNull() )
07463         {
07464             // on récupère les deux couleurs de chaque liste a partir des deux widgets de la fenêtre d'évaluation
07465 
07466             // les listes des points seront constitués de la position des pixels ayant ces couleurs
07467 
07468             unsigned char redA, greenA, blueA;
07469 
07470             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 0 )
07471             {
07472                 redA = 255;
07473                 greenA = 0;
07474                 blueA = 0;
07475             }
07476             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 1 )
07477             {
07478                 redA = 0;
07479                 greenA = 255;
07480                 blueA = 0;
07481             }
07482             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 2 )
07483             {
07484                 redA = 0;
07485                 greenA = 0;
07486                 blueA = 255;
07487             }
07488             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 3 )
07489             {
07490                 redA = 0;
07491                 greenA = 255;
07492                 blueA = 255;
07493             }
07494             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 4 )
07495             {
07496                 redA = 255;
07497                 greenA = 0;
07498                 blueA = 255;
07499             }
07500             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 5 )
07501             {
07502                 redA = 255;
07503                 greenA = 255;
07504                 blueA = 0;
07505             }
07506             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 6 )
07507             {
07508                 redA = 0;
07509                 greenA = 0;
07510                 blueA = 0;
07511             }
07512             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 7 )
07513             {
07514                 redA = 255;
07515                 greenA = 255;
07516                 blueA = 255;
07517             }
07518             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 8 )
07519             {
07520                 redA = redAselected;
07521                 greenA = greenAselected;
07522                 blueA = blueAselected;
07523             }
07524 
07525             unsigned char redB, greenB, blueB;
07526 
07527             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 0 )
07528             {
07529                 redB = 255;
07530                 greenB = 0;
07531                 blueB = 0;
07532             }
07533             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 1 )
07534             {
07535                 redB = 0;
07536                 greenB = 255;
07537                 blueB = 0;
07538             }
07539             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 2 )
07540             {
07541                 redB = 0;
07542                 greenB = 0;
07543                 blueB = 255;
07544             }
07545             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 3 )
07546             {
07547                 redB = 0;
07548                 greenB = 255;
07549                 blueB = 255;
07550             }
07551             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 4 )
07552             {
07553                 redB = 255;
07554                 greenB = 0;
07555                 blueB = 255;
07556             }
07557             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 5 )
07558             {
07559                 redB = 255;
07560                 greenB = 255;
07561                 blueB = 0;
07562             }
07563             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 6 )
07564             {
07565                 redB = 0;
07566                 greenB = 0;
07567                 blueB = 0;
07568             }
07569             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 7 )
07570             {
07571                 redB = 255;
07572                 greenB = 255;
07573                 blueB = 255;
07574             }
07575             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 8 )
07576             {
07577                 redB = redBselected;
07578                 greenB = greenBselected;
07579                 blueB = blueBselected;
07580             }
07581 
07582 
07583             // détermination de la taille des listes
07584 
07585             int listA_length = 0;
07586             int listB_length = 0;
07587 
07588             QRgb pix;
07589 
07590             int i, x, y; // offset and position
07591 
07592             for( i = 0; i < imgA_size; i++ )
07593             {
07594                 // i = x+y*imgA_width so
07595                 y = i/imgA_width;
07596                 x = i-y*imgA_width;
07597 
07598                 pix = image1.pixel(x,y);
07599 
07600                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix))==redA && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix))==greenA && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix)==blueA) )
07601                 {
07602                     listA_length++;
07603                 }
07604             }
07605 
07606             for( i = 0; i < imgB_size; i++ )
07607             {
07608                 // i = x+y*imgB_width so
07609                 y = i/imgB_width;
07610                 x = i-y*imgB_width;
07611 
07612                 pix = image2.pixel(x,y);
07613 
07614                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix)) == redB && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix)) == greenB && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix) == blueB) )
07615                 {
07616                     listB_length++;
07617                 }
07618             }
07619 
07620             // on déclare les pointeurs et alloue la mémoire de chaque liste en fonction de leur taille
07621 
07622             int* listA = new int[listA_length];
07623             int* listB = new int[listB_length];
07624 
07625 
07626             // on remplit les listes
07627 
07628             int index1 = 0;
07629             int index2 = 0;
07630 
07631             for( i = 0; i < imgA_size; i++ )
07632             {
07633                 y = i/imgA_width;
07634                 x = i-y*imgA_width;
07635 
07636                 pix = image1.pixel(x,y);
07637 
07638                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix)) == redA && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix)) == greenA && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix) == blueA) )
07639                 {
07640                     listA[index1] = i;
07641                     index1++;
07642                 }
07643             }
07644 
07645             for( i = 0; i < imgB_size; i++ )
07646             {
07647                 y = i/imgB_width;
07648                 x = i-y*imgB_width;
07649 
07650                 pix = image2.pixel(x,y);
07651 
07652                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix)) == redB && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix)) == greenB && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix) == blueB) )
07653                 {
07654                     listB[index2] = i;
07655                     index2++;
07656                 }
07657             }
07658 
07659 
07660             // création d'un objet a partir des listes
07661             ofeli::HausdorffDistance hausdorffDistance1(listA, listA_length, imgA_width, imgA_height, listB, listB_length, imgB_width, imgB_height);
07662 
07663             // utilisation des accesseurs
07664             double hausdorff_dist1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_hausdorff_dist();
07665             double modified_hausdorff_dist1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_modified_hausdorff_dist();
07666             double hausdorff_ratio1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_hausdorff_ratio();
07667             double modified_hausdorff_ratio1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_modified_hausdorff_ratio();
07668             double centers_dist1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_centers_dist();
07669             double centers_ratio1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_centers_ratio();
07670 
07671             // affichage
07672             if( listA_length != 0 && listB_length != 0 )
07673             {
07674                 label_hausdorff->setText(tr("Hausdorff distance = ")+QString::number(hausdorff_dist1)+(tr(" pixels")));
07675                 label_hausdorff_ratio->setText(tr("Hausdorff ratio = ")+QString::number(100.0*hausdorff_ratio1)+(" %"));
07676                 label_modified_hausdorff->setText(tr("modified Hausdorff distance = ")+QString::number(modified_hausdorff_dist1)+(tr(" pixels")));
07677                 label_modified_hausdorff_ratio->setText(tr("modified Hausdorff ratio = ")+QString::number(100.0*modified_hausdorff_ratio1)+(" %"));
07678                 label_centers_dist->setText(tr("distance between centers = ")+QString::number(centers_dist1)+(tr(" pixels")));
07679                 label_centers_ratio->setText(tr("ratio between centers = ")+QString::number(100.0*centers_ratio1)+(" %"));
07680             }
07681             else
07682             {
07683                 QString error_msg1;
07684                 QString error_msg2;
07685                 if( listA_length == 0 && listB_length == 0 )
07686                 {
07687                     error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The lists A and B are empty."));
07688                     error_msg2 = (tr("Change the lists colors."));
07689                 }
07690                 if( listA_length == 0 && listB_length != 0 )
07691                 {
07692                     error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The list A is empty."));
07693                     error_msg2 = (tr("Change the list A color."));
07694                 }
07695                 if( listA_length != 0 && listB_length == 0 )
07696                 {
07697                     error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The list B is empty."));
07698                     error_msg2 = (tr("Change the list B color."));
07699                 }
07700 
07701                 label_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
07702                 label_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
07703                 label_modified_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
07704                 label_modified_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
07705                 label_centers_dist->setText(error_msg1);
07706                 label_centers_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
07707             }
07708 
07709             // on supprime les listes
07710             delete[] listA;
07711             delete[] listB;
07712         }
07713 
07714         else
07715         {
07716             QString error_msg1;
07717             QString error_msg2;
07718             if( image1.isNull() && image2.isNull() )
07719             {
07720                 error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The images A and B are not open."));
07721                 error_msg2 = (tr("Open image A and image B."));
07722             }
07723             if( image1.isNull() && !image2.isNull() )
07724             {
07725                 error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The image A is not open."));
07726                 error_msg2 = (tr("Open image A."));
07727             }
07728             if( !image1.isNull() && image2.isNull() )
07729             {
07730                 error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The image B is not open."));
07731                 error_msg2 = (tr("Open image B."));
07732             }
07733 
07734             label_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
07735             label_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
07736             label_modified_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
07737             label_modified_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
07738             label_centers_dist->setText(error_msg1);
07739             label_centers_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
07740         }
07741     }
07742 }

08012 void ImageViewer::openFilenamePhi()
08013 {
08014     fileName_phi = QFileDialog::getOpenFileName(this,
08015                                             tr("Open File"),
08016                                             last_directory_used,
08017                                             tr("Image Files (%1)").arg(nameFilters.join(" ")));
08018

08021 
08022 void ImageViewer::open_phi()
08023 {
08024     if( img1 != NULL )
08025     {
08026         if( !fileName_phi.isEmpty() )
08027         {
08028             QFileInfo fi(fileName_phi);
08029             last_directory_used = fi.absolutePath();
08030 
08031             QImage img_phi1 = QImage(fileName_phi);
08032 
08033             if( img_phi1.isNull() )
08034             {
08035                 QMessageBox::information(this, tr("Opening error - Ofeli"),
08036                                          tr("Cannot load %1.").arg(fileName_phi));
08037                 return;
08038             }
08039 
08040             img_phi1 = img_phi1.convertToFormat(QImage::Format_RGB888);
08041             img_phi1 = img_phi1.scaled(img_width, img_height, Qt::IgnoreAspectRatio, Qt::FastTransformation);
08042 
08043             QRgb pix;
08044 
08045             int i, x, y; // offset and position
08046 
08047             for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
08048             {
08049                 // i = x+y*img_width so
08050                 y = i/img_width;
08051                 x = i-y*img_width;
08052 
08053                 pix = img_phi1.pixel(x,y);
08054 
08055                 if( (0.2989*(double)(qRed(pix)) + 0.5870*(double)(qGreen(pix)) + 0.1140*(double)(qBlue(pix)) ) < 128.0 )
08056                 {
08057                     phi_init1[i] = 1;
08058                     phi_init2[i] = 1;
08059                 }
08060                 else
08061                 {
08062                     phi_init1[i] = -1;
08063                     phi_init2[i] = -1;
08064                 }
08065 
08066             }
08067 
08068             clean_boundaries(phi_init1,phi_init1_clean);
08069             clean_boundaries(phi_init2,phi_init2_clean);
08070 
08071             QSettings settings;
08072 
08073             settings.setValue("Settings/Initialization/img_phi", img_phi1);
08074         }
08075 
08076         tab_visu(onglets->currentIndex());
08077     }
08078 }
08079 
08080 void ImageViewer::save_phi()
08081 {
08082     if( phi_init2_clean != NULL )
08083     {
08084         QImage img_phi_save = QImage(img_width,img_height, QImage::Format_RGB888);
08085 
08086         int i, x, y; // offset and position
08087 
08088         for( i = 0; i < img_size; i++ )
08089         {
08090             // i = x+y*img_width so
08091             y = i/img_width;
08092             x = i-y*img_width;
08093 
08094             if( phi_init2_clean[i] > 0 )
08095             {
08096                 img_phi_save.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(0,0,0));
08097             }
08098             else
08099             {
08100                 img_phi_save.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(255,255,255));
08101             }
08102         }
08103 
08104         QString fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
08105                                                              tr("Save ϕ(t=0)"),
08106                                                              last_directory_used + QString(tr("/initial_phi.png")),
08107                                                              "PNG (*.png)");
08108         // sauvegarde
08109         img_phi_save.save(fileName_save);
08110     }
08111 }

08249 void ImageViewer::setCurrentFile(const QString &fileName1)
08250 {
08251     curFile = fileName1;
08252     //setWindowFilePath(curFile);
08253 
08254     QSettings settings;
08255     QStringList files = settings.value("name/recentFileList").toStringList();
08256     files.removeAll(fileName1);
08257     files.prepend(fileName1);
08258     while( files.size() > MaxRecentFiles )
08259     {
08260         files.removeLast();
08261     }
08262 
08263     settings.setValue("name/recentFileList", files);
08264 
08265     foreach( QWidget *widget, QApplication::topLevelWidgets() )
08266     {
08267         ImageViewer *imageViewer = qobject_cast<ImageViewer *>(widget);
08268         if( imageViewer )
08269         {
08270             imageViewer->updateRecentFileActions();
08271         }
08272     }
08273 }
08274 
08275 void ImageViewer::updateRecentFileActions()
08276 {
08277     QSettings settings;
08278     QStringList files = settings.value("name/recentFileList").toStringList();
08279 
08280     int numRecentFiles = qMin(files.size(), (int)MaxRecentFiles);
08281 
08282     for( int i = 0; i < numRecentFiles; ++i )
08283     {
08284         QString text = tr("&%1   %2").arg(i + 1).arg( strippedName(files[i]) );
08285         recentFileActs[i]->setText(text);
08286         recentFileActs[i]->setData(files[i]);
08287         recentFileActs[i]->setVisible(true);
08288     }
08289 
08290     for( int j = numRecentFiles; j < MaxRecentFiles; ++j )
08291     {
08292         recentFileActs[j]->setVisible(false);
08293     }
08294 
08295     separatorAct->setVisible(numRecentFiles > 0);
08296 
08297     if( files.isEmpty() )
08298     {
08299         deleteAct->setVisible(false);
08300     }
08301     else
08302     {
08303         deleteAct->setVisible(true);
08304     }
08305 }
08306 
08307 QString ImageViewer::strippedName(const QString &fullFileName)
08308 {
08309     return QFileInfo(fullFileName).fileName();
08310 }
08311 
08312 void ImageViewer::openRecentFile()
08313 {
08314     QAction* action = qobject_cast<QAction*>( sender() );
08315     if( action )
08316     {
08317         fileName = action->data().toString();
08318     }
08319 
08320     open();
08321 }
08322 
08323 void ImageViewer::deleteList()
08324 {
08325     QStringList files;
08326     files.clear();
08327 
08328     QSettings settings;
08329     settings.setValue("name/recentFileList", files);
08330 
08331     updateRecentFileActions();
08332 }
